âœ¦ Now that the resiter imports are fixed, I will address the E0118: no nominal type found for inherent implementation errors. These
  errors occur because impl<D: Dataset> D is an inherent implementation on a generic type parameter D, which is not allowed in Rust.
  The methods need to be implemented directly on the Dataset trait itself, or on a concrete type that implements Dataset.

  Since we are refactoring sophia_api, the correct approach is to move these methods back into the Dataset trait definition in
  dataset_trait.rs and Graph trait definition in graph_trait.rs.

  I will start with dataset_trait.rs. I will read the content of dataset_trait.rs and then add the methods back into the pub trait
  Dataset block.
 â•­â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â•®

 â”‚     4                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     5 # SOP: Branching Strategy                                                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚     6                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     7 ## 1. Objective                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     8 To define a clear and consistent branching strategy for the `ragit` project, facilitating isolated                          â”‚
 â”‚       development, effective collaboration, and robust integration, especially when dealing with nested submodules                â”‚
 â”‚       and complex dependency fixes.                                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚     9                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    10 ## 2. Core Principles                                                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚    11 - **Isolation**: All new features, bug fixes, or significant refactoring efforts should be developed on                     â”‚
 â”‚       dedicated branches.                                                                                                         â”‚
 â”‚    12 - **Hierarchy**: For work involving submodules, create branches within the submodule itself to isolate changes              â”‚
 â”‚       specific to that submodule.                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚    13 - **Traceability**: Ensure all work is committed with descriptive messages and documented in relevant quality               â”‚
 â”‚       procedures or work logs.                                                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚    14                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    15 ## 3. Branch Naming Conventions                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    16 - **Feature Branches (Main Repository)**: `feature/<descriptive-name>` (e.g.,                                               â”‚
 â”‚       `feature/dyim-embedding-pipeline`)                                                                                          â”‚
 â”‚    17 - **Bugfix Branches (Main Repository)**: `bugfix/<issue-id>-<descriptive-name>` (e.g.,                                      â”‚
 â”‚       `bugfix/GH-123-fix-auth-flow`)                                                                                              â”‚
 â”‚    18 - **Submodule Branches**: `<submodule-name>-<descriptive-name>` (e.g., `sophia-rs-compat-fix`)                              â”‚
 â”‚    19                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    20 ## 4. Procedure                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    21                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    22 ### Step 1: Create a Main Feature/Bugfix Branch                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    23 - For any new development or bug fix in the main `ragit` repository, create a new branch from `main` (or                    â”‚
 â”‚       `develop`, if applicable).                                                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚    24 - **Command:** `git checkout -b <branch-name>`                                                                              â”‚
 â”‚    25                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    26 ### Step 2: Identify Submodule Involvement                                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚    27 - Determine if the work requires modifications within any nested Git submodules (e.g.,                                      â”‚
 â”‚       `vendor/meta-introspector/solfunmeme-dioxus/vendor/sophia_rs/`).                                                            â”‚
 â”‚    28                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    29 ### Step 3: Create a Submodule-Specific Branch (if applicable)                                                              â”‚
 â”‚    30 - If a submodule is involved, navigate into the submodule's directory.                                                      â”‚
 â”‚    31 - Create a new branch within that submodule to isolate changes specific to it.                                              â”‚
 â”‚    32 - **Command:** `git -C <path/to/submodule> checkout -b <submodule-branch-name>`                                             â”‚
 â”‚    33                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    34 ### Step 4: Commit Changes within Submodule                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚    35 - Perform all necessary modifications within the submodule.                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚    36 - Stage and commit these changes *within the submodule's repository*.                                                       â”‚
 â”‚    37 - **Command (from main repo root):** `git -C <path/to/submodule> add .`                                                     â”‚
 â”‚    38 - **Command (from main repo root):** `git -C <path/to/submodule> commit -m "<descriptive-commit-message>"`                  â”‚
 â”‚    39                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    40 ### Step 5: Update Main Repository's Submodule Reference                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚    41 - After committing changes in the submodule, the main repository's reference to that submodule will be                      â”‚
 â”‚       updated.                                                                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚    42 - Stage and commit this updated submodule reference in the main repository.                                                 â”‚
 â”‚    43 - **Command (from main repo root):** `git add <path/to/submodule>`                                                          â”‚
 â”‚    44 - **Command (from main repo root):** `git commit -m "Update <submodule-name> to <new-commit-hash>"`                         â”‚
 â”‚    45                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    46 ### Step 6: Integrate Submodule Branch (Optional, for specific scenarios)                                                   â”‚
 â”‚    47 - In some cases, it might be necessary to branch off an older version of a submodule (e.g., to apply a fix to               â”‚
 â”‚       a specific release or to isolate a compatibility layer).                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚    48 - **Command (from submodule directory):** `git checkout -b <new-branch-name> <older-commit-hash>`                           â”‚
 â”‚    49 - **Note:** This creates a detached HEAD state in the submodule. Ensure you understand the implications and                 â”‚
 â”‚       manage the submodule's state carefully.                                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚    50                                                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚    51 ## 5. Documentation                                                                                                         â”‚
 â”‚    52 - All significant branching decisions and their rationale should be documented in the relevant work logs                    â”‚
 â”‚       (e.g., `dyim_embedding_pipeline_work_log.md`).                                                                              â”‚
 â”‚    53 - New SOPs should be linked from `docs/index.md`.                                                                           â”‚
